Yo Derek! I heard you talking about your sleep apnea and possible deviated septum. I am not qualified but I believe those are actually symptoms of a poorly formed jaw.   Basically the food of modernity is too soft so when we are growing up there isn't enough stress placed on the facial muscles (and orthodontics recess the mandible) so the muscles form down and back into the throat. I think you have some sort of malocclusion (I do too) of the jaw, which is also a cause of teeth grinding.  Some resources I've turned to to learn about this is the YouTube Page "Jaw Hacks" and the book "Jaws: The Story of a Hidden Epidemic" by Sandra Kahn and Paul Erlich
